  <script>
   /*********************/
    /** Check UserAgent **/
    /*********************/
    function addCss(url)
    {
        var link = document.createElement('link');
        link.rel  = 'stylesheet';
        link.type = 'text/css';
        link.href = url;
        link.media = 'all';
        var head = document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
        head.appendChild(link);
    }

    var ua = navigator.userAgent,
        doc = document.documentElement;

    var useragent = (ua.match(/MSIE 10.0/i)) ? 'ie10' :
                    (ua.match(/rv:11.0/i)) ? 'ie11' :
                    (ua.match(/Firefox/i)) ? 'ff' :
                    (ua.match(/Chrome/i)) ? 'chrome' :
                    (ua.match(/Opera/i)) ? 'opera' :
                    (ua.match(/Safari/i)) ? 'safari' :
                        'other';

    doc.setAttribute('data-useragent', useragent);
    if (useragent.match(/ie/i)) {
        addCss('http://www.magentocommerce.com/magento-connect/skin/frontend/enterprise/mc/css/styles-ie10+.css');
//uncomment bellow in case if you need styles, which cannot be added to styles-ie10+.css
//        addCss('http://www.magentocommerce.com/magento-connect/skin/frontend/enterprise/connect/css'+'/styles-ie'+document.documentMode+'.css');
    }

    var BrowserDetect =
    {
        init: function () {
            this.browser = this.searchString(this.dataBrowser) || "Other";
            this.version = this.searchVersion(navigator.userAgent) || this.searchVersion(navigator.appVersion) || "Unknown";
        },

        /**
         * Get browser name
         *
         * @param {string} data
         * @returns {string}
         */
        searchString: function (data) {
            for (var i = 0; i &lt; data.length; i++) {
                var dataString = data[i].string;
                this.versionSearchString = data[i].subString;

                if (dataString.indexOf(data[i].subString) != -1) {
                    return data[i].identity;
                }
            }
        },

        /**
         * Get browser version
         * @param {string} dataString
         * @returns {Number}
         */
        searchVersion: function (dataString) {
            var index = dataString.indexOf(this.versionSearchString);
            if (index == -1) return;
            return parseFloat(dataString.substring(index + this.versionSearchString.length + 1));
        },

        dataBrowser: [
            { string: navigator.userAgent, subString: "Chrome", identity: "Chrome" },
            { string: navigator.userAgent, subString: "MSIE", identity: "Explorer" },
            { string: navigator.userAgent, subString: "Trident", identity: "Explorer" },
            { string: navigator.userAgent, subString: "Firefox", identity: "Firefox" },
            { string: navigator.userAgent, subString: "Safari", identity: "Safari" },
            { string: navigator.userAgent, subString: "Opera", identity: "Opera" }
        ]

    };
    BrowserDetect.init();
  </script>

        <script type="text/javascript">
         var searchFormWidget = {
        searchFormObj: null,
        searchForm: $('extension_search_form'),
        searchField: $('extension_search_keywords'),
        searchButton: $('extension_search_button'),
        defaultSerchText: 'Search for Extensions',
        forbiddenCharacter: ["|"],
        /**
         * Create VarienForm obj, bind observers
         */
        init: function() {
            this.searchFormObj = new VarienForm('extension_search_form', false);
            // IE9 hack
            //this.searchForm.observe('submit', this.onSubmitForm.bind(this));
            this.searchButton.observe('click', this.onButtonClick.bind(this));
            this.searchField.observe('keydown', this.onInputKeyDown.bind(this));
            this.searchField.observe('focus', this.onInputFocus.bind(this));
            this.searchField.observe('blur', this.onInputBlur.bind(this));
        },
        /**
         * Submit form validation passed
         */
        submitForm: function() {
            this.searchField.value = this.sanitizeKeyword(this.searchField.value);
            if (this.searchField.value == this.defaultSerchText) {
                this.searchField.value = '';
            }
            var keywords = this.searchField.value;
            gaTracker.trackMainSearchEvent(keywords);
            setTimeout(function() { searchFormWidget.searchFormObj.submit() }, 500);
        },
        /**
         * Action bound on form submit
         */
        /**
         * Action bound on button click event
         */
        onButtonClick: function(event) {
            event.preventDefault();
            this.submitForm();
        },
        /**
         * Action bound on search field when 'Enter' pressed
         */
        onInputKeyDown: function(event) {
            if (event.keyCode == Event.KEY_RETURN) {
                event.preventDefault();
                this.submitForm();
            }
        },
        /**
         * Action bound on search field focus event
         */
        onInputFocus: function(event) {
            if (this.searchField.value==this.defaultSerchText) {
                this.searchField.value='';
            }
        },
        /**
         * Action bound on search field blur event
         */
        onInputBlur: function(event) {
            if (this.searchField.value == '') {
                this.searchField.value = this.defaultSerchText;
            }
        },
        /**
         * Remove forbidden characters
         */
        sanitizeKeyword: function(keyword) {
            this.forbiddenCharacter.each(function(character) {
                var reg = new RegExp('\\' + character, 'g');
                keyword = keyword.replace(reg, ' ');
            });
            keyword = keyword.replace(/\s+/g, ' ');
            keyword = keyword.strip();

            return keyword;
        }
    };
    searchFormWidget.init();

        jQuery( document ).ready(function( $ ) {
        $( "#extension_search_keywords" ).autocomplete({
            source: 'http://www.magentocommerce.com/magento-connect/suggester/',
            minLength: 2,
            delay: 500,
            appendTo: "#search-auto-suggest",
            open: function() {
              var position = $("#search-auto-suggest").position(),
                  left = position.left, top = position.top, width =  $("#search-auto-suggest").width();

              $("#search-auto-suggest &gt; ul").css({left: (left + 36) + "px",
                top: (top + 66) + "px" }).width(width - 11);

            }
        }).data( "ui-autocomplete" )._renderItem = function( ul, item ) {
            return $( "&lt;li&gt;" )
                .append( "&lt;a&gt;&lt;span&gt;" + item.label + "&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;" )
                .appendTo( ul );
        };
    });
        </script>
       </div>
       <div id="search-auto-suggest">
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>

        <script type="text/javascript">

          <script type="text/javascript">
           //script for a long price
        jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
            var priceWrapper = $('#extension-price-wrap'),
                price = $('#extension-price', priceWrapper),
                trustedExtensionIcon = $('#trusted-extension'),
                widthLimit,
                diff = 2;

            var timer = setTimeout(function() {
                trustedExtensionIcon ? widthLimit = priceWrapper.width() - trustedExtensionIcon.width() : widthLimit = price.width();
                var coef = widthLimit / price.width(),
                    priceFontSize = parseInt(price.css('fontSize'));

                if (BrowserDetect.browser == 'Explorer' &amp;&amp; BrowserDetect.version == 7) {
                    priceFontSize = 26;
                    if (!trustedExtensionIcon.length &amp;&amp; price.width() &gt; 170) {
                        price.css({
                            'fontSize': 24 + 'px'
                        });
                    }
                }

                if (coef &lt; 1) {
                    price.css({
                        'width': widthLimit + 'px',
                        'fontSize': (priceFontSize - diff) * coef + 'px'
                    });
                }
            }, 200);
        }(jQuery));
          </script>

      <div id="product-view-tabs">
       <script type="text/javascript">
        window.onload = function() {
    var goEditionIds = {"3":"3"};
    var select = $('available_edition_edition_id');
    var note = $('product-view-tabs-notification');
    var options = $('available_edition_edition_id').getElementsBySelector('option');
    var noteToggle = function(e){
        this.checked = false;
        var _this = this;
        options.each(function(item) {
            if (_this.checked) {
                return;
            }
            if (item.selected &amp;&amp; goEditionIds[item.value] == item.value) {
                note.hide();
                _this.checked = true;
            }
        });
        if (!this.checked) {
            note.show();
        }
    };
    Event.observe(select, 'change', noteToggle);
    noteToggle();
}
       </script>
       <div id="product-view-tabs-notification" style="display: none;">
        Please note that this extension is provided as is. It is recommended to always backup your installation prior to use.
       </div>
       <dl class="ui-tabs clearfix">
        <dt class="tab-description">
         Overview
        </dt>
        <dd class="tab-content-description">
         <div class="clearfix">
          <div class="std" itemprop="description">
           <div id="product-view-tabs-branding">
           </div>
           <h2>
            MageMob Admin
           </h2>
           <p>
            MageMob Admin allows online merchants to view all the details of their online store on their iOS and Android Tab. The extension helps store owners to view stores order details, product details, customers details anywhere and anytime with help of their iOS/Android Tab. This extension eliminates the need to login from PC to get detailed information of the happenings in online stores.
           </p>
           <p>
            MageMob Admin integrates with your online store and delivers the key details to your iOS/Android Tab. You can easily navigate through the orders, products, customers and sales report from your handheld device and monitor the performance of your store wherever you go.
           </p>
           <h3>
            Features of Mobile Assistant:
           </h3>
           <ul>
            <li>
             Easy to use and quick to install
            </li>
            <li>
             Supported by Multiple store websites
            </li>
            <li>
             Filters order, product, and sales with respect to a particular store
            </li>
            <li>
             Displays order details with status  Successfully delivered, pending, back order etc.
            </li>
            <li>
             Displays product list and products details
            </li>
            <li>
             Displays customer list, details, address and shipping address
            </li>
            <li>
             Sends notification to the store merchant as soon as a new order is placed with its details
            </li>
            <li>
             Customized dashboard that displays store wise sales graphs that can be filtered days wise  7 days, 30 days or 90 days
            </li>
           </ul>
           <strong>
            Note:  Apple notification working  on PHP 5.3.0 or later.
           </strong>
           <p>

     <script type="text/javascript">
      var BVReviewLanguagesSwitcher = {
        // Properties
        tooltipMessage: 'You can choose one of these languages to write Review for Extension',
        // use a selector instead a jquery object because the placeholder may be dynamic (in child objects)
        languageSwitcherPlaceholderSelector: '#BVSubmissionReviewContainer',
        submissionContainer: jQuery('#BVSubmissionReviewContainer'),
        languagesMap: {"4643-en_gb":"English","4643-de_de":"German","4643-es_es":"Spanish","4643-zh_cn":"Chinese","4643-pt_pt":"Portuguese","4643-fr_fr":"French","4643-nl_nl":"Dutch","4643-ru_ru":"Russian","4643-it_it":"Italian","4643-ja_jp":"Japanese"},
        entityId: '20061',
        namespace: 'reviews',
        languageSwitcherWrapper: null,
        languageCode: null,

        // Methods
        handleLanguageSwitcher: function(pageType) {
            switch (pageType) {
                case 'Input':
                    // Create language selector if it's doesn't exist
                    if (null === document.getElementById('opinion-ui-language-' + this.namespace)) {
                        this.buildSwitcher();
                    } else {
                        this.showSwitcher();
                    }
                    break;
                case 'Preview':
                    if (this.languageSwitcherWrapper) {
                        this.hideSwitcher();
                    }
                    break;
                case 'Confirm':
                case 'Cancel':
                    if (this.languageSwitcherWrapper) {
                        this.removeSwitcher();
                    }
                    break;
            }

            return this;
        },
        buildSwitcher: function() {
            // place language selector into DOM
            this.languageSwitcherWrapper = jQuery(this.getLanguagesHtml());
            this.languageSwitcherWrapper.insertBefore(jQuery(this.languageSwitcherPlaceholderSelector));
            // style language selector through Niceforms plugin
            Niceforms.init();

            var self = this;
            jQuery('#BVLanguageSwitcher-' + this.namespace).bind('change', function() {
                if (jQuery(this).val() != self.languageCode) {
                    self.languageCode = jQuery(this).val();
                    self.reloadBVSubmitForm(self.languageCode);
                }
            });

            // for editing after preview
            if (self.languageCode != null) {
                self.toggleLanguage(self.languageCode);
            }

            return this;
        },
        toggleLanguage: function(languageCode) {
            var languageLabel = this.languagesMap[languageCode];

            this.languageSwitcherWrapper.find('div.select span').attr('title', languageLabel).text(languageLabel);
            this.languageSwitcherWrapper.find('div.options ul li.selected').removeClass('selected').parent()
                .find('li span[title="' + languageLabel + '"]').parent().addClass('selected');

            return this;
        },
        reloadBVSubmitForm: function(languageCode) {
            this.submissionContainer.empty();

            var self = this;
            $BV.ui('rr', 'submit_review', {
                productId: self.entityId,
                displayCode: languageCode,
                onEvent: function(json) {
                    self.handleLanguageSwitcher(json.pageType);
                }
            });

            return this;
        },
        getLanguagesHtml: function() {
            var html = '\
                &lt;div id="opinion-ui-language-' + this.namespace + '" class="opinion-ui-language nice-form"&gt;\
                Choose your language:\
                &lt;select id="BVLanguageSwitcher-' + this.namespace + '"&gt;';

            for (var langCode in this.languagesMap) {
                html += '&lt;option value="' + langCode + '"&gt;' + this.languagesMap[langCode] + '&lt;/option&gt;';
            }

            html += '&lt;/select&gt;\
                &lt;span class="ui-tooltip-question"&gt;\
                    &lt;span class="ui-tooltip"&gt;\
                        &lt;b&gt;Language Preferences&lt;/b&gt;\
                        &lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;' + this.tooltipMessage + '&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;\
                    &lt;/span&gt;\
                &lt;/span&gt;\
                &lt;/div&gt;';

            return html;
        },
        showSwitcher: function() {
            this.languageSwitcherWrapper.show();

            return this;
        },
        hideSwitcher: function() {
            this.languageSwitcherWrapper.hide();

            return this;
        },
        removeSwitcher: function() {
            this.languageSwitcherWrapper.remove();
            this.languageCode = null;

            return this;
        }
    };

    var BVReplyLanguagesSwitcher = jQuery.extend({}, BVReviewLanguagesSwitcher, {
        tooltipMessage: 'You can choose one of these languages to write Comment for Review',
        languageSwitcherPlaceholderSelector: '#BVDivCommentAndInformationSectionID',
        parentId: null,
        reloadBVSubmitForm: function(languageCode) {
            this.submissionContainer.empty();

            var self = this;
            $BV.ui('rr', 'submit_comment', {
                productId: self.entityId,
                reviewId: self.parentId,
                displayCode: languageCode,
                onEvent: function(json) {
                    self.handleLanguageSwitcher(json.pageType);
                }
            });

            return this;
        },
        setParentId: function(parentId) {
            this.parentId = parentId;

            return this;
        }
    });

    $BV.configure('global', {
        allowSamePageSubmission: true,
        userToken: "",
        doLogin: function(successCallback, successUrl) {
            customerAuthorization.popupOpen('#authorization-popup-login-form', {
                url: 'http://www.magentocommerce.com/magento-connect/appstore_bv/index/redirect/?bvreturn=' + encodeURIComponent(successUrl)
            });
        }
    });

    $BV.configure('rr', {
        submissionContainerDiv: 'BVSubmissionReviewContainer',
        doShowSubmission: function() {
            $('BVRRContainer').hide();
            this.doShowContent();
        },
        onSubmissionReturn: function() {
            // we don't know what a form(review or reply) has been canceled
            BVReviewLanguagesSwitcher.handleLanguageSwitcher('Cancel');
            BVReplyLanguagesSwitcher.handleLanguageSwitcher('Cancel');

            jQuery('#BVSubmissionReviewContainer').empty();
            jQuery('#BVRRContainer').show();
        },
        doScrollSubmission: function() {
            $('BVSubmissionReviewContainer').scrollTo();
            return false;
        },
        doShowContent: function() {
            var tabDt = jQuery('dt.tab-product\\.bv\\.reviews').eq(0);
            if (tabDt &amp;&amp; !tabDt.hasClass('active')) {
                tabDt.trigger('click');
            }
        }
    });

    $BV.ui('rr', 'show_reviews', {
        productId: '20061',
        onEvent: function(json) {
            if (json.attributes.avgRating || !json.attributes.numReviews) {
                jQuery('#opinion-developer-about').show();
            }

            if ('Comment' === json.eventTarget) {
                BVReplyLanguagesSwitcher.setParentId(json.attributes.ugcOnPage[0].id)
                    .handleLanguageSwitcher(json.pageType);
            } else {
                BVReviewLanguagesSwitcher.handleLanguageSwitcher(json.pageType);
            }
        }
    });
     </script>
    </div>

                  <div class="BVQAContent BVQAAnswer BVDI_BAContentTop10Contributor" id="BVQAAnswer526144">
                   <div class="BVQAContentData BVAnswerData">
                    <div class="BVQASignature">
                     <span class="BVQAAvatar">
                      <span class="BVQALinkSpan">
                       <img alt="Customer avatar" src="http://magento.ugc.bazaarvoice.com/answers/4643-en_us/static/noAvatar.gif" title="Customer avatar"/>
                      </span>

                     <div class="BVQAContentText BVQAAnswerText">
                      <div class="BVQAContentLabel BVQAAnswerLabel">
                       Answer:
                      </div>
                      Hello Dear,
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      Greetings from Biztech, Thanks for asking this, we are happy to assist you.
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      It seems that extension/extension URL is not configured properly in your device.
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      1. Just make sure you have configured extension properly . Soap Users are created and roles have been assigned to them.
                      <br/>
                      2. Once Try cleaning magento cache from admin and then again try to check with your device.
                      <br/>
                      3. While configuring in your device make sure you have entered proper URL. Like http://www.yourwebsiteurl.com/index.php and if its https https://www.yourwebsiteurl.com/index.php
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      After doing all above if you still facing any issue please sent over email to support@biztechconsultancy.com we will assist you further on this.
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      Thanks,
                     </div>

                     <div class="BVQAContentText BVQAAnswerText">
                      <div class="BVQAContentLabel BVQAAnswerLabel">
                       Answer:
                      </div>
                      Hello Dear,
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      Thanks for asking this, we are happy to assist you.
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      1. Just make sure you have configured extension properly . Soap Users are created and roles have been assigned to them.
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      2. Once Try cleaning magento cache from admin and then again try to check with your device.
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      3. While configuring in your device make sure you have entered proper URL. Like http://www.yourwebsiteurl.com/index.php and if its https https://www.yourwebsiteurl.com/index.php
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      After doing all above if you still facing any issue please sent over email @ support@biztechconsultancy.com . we will assist you further on this.
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      Thanks,
                     </div>

      <script type="text/javascript">
       var BVQuestionLanguagesSwitcher = jQuery.extend({}, BVReviewLanguagesSwitcher, {
        tooltipMessage: 'You can choose one of these languages to write Question for Extension',
        // use a selector instead a jquery object because the placeholder may be dynamic (in child objects)
        languageSwitcherPlaceholderSelector: '#BVSubmissionQaContainer',
        submissionContainer: jQuery('#BVSubmissionQaContainer'),
        namespace: 'qa',
        reloadBVSubmitForm: function(languageCode) {
            this.submissionContainer.empty();

            var self = this;
            $BV.ui('qa', 'submit_question', {
                subjectType: 'product',
                productId: '20061',
                displayCode: languageCode,
                onEvent: function(json) {
                    self.handleLanguageSwitcher(json.pageType);
                }
            });

            return this;
        }
    });

    var BVAnswerLanguagesSwitcher = jQuery.extend({}, BVQuestionLanguagesSwitcher, {
        tooltipMessage: 'You can choose one of these languages to write Answer for Question',
        languageSwitcherPlaceholderSelector: '#BVDivAnswerAndInformationSectionID',
        parentId: null,
        reloadBVSubmitForm: function(languageCode) {
            this.submissionContainer.empty();

            var self = this;
            $BV.ui('qa', 'submit_answer', {
                subjectType: 'product',
                productId: self.entityId,
                questionId: self.parentId,
                displayCode: languageCode,
                onEvent: function(json) {
                    self.handleLanguageSwitcher(json.pageType);
                }
            });

            return this;
        },
        setParentId: function(parentId) {
            this.parentId = parentId;

            return this;
        }
    });

    $BV.configure('qa', {
        submissionContainerDiv: 'BVSubmissionQaContainer',
        doShowSubmission: function() {
            $('BVQAContainer').hide();
            this.doShowContent();
        },
        onSubmissionReturn: function() {
            // we don't know what a form(question or answer) has been canceled
            BVQuestionLanguagesSwitcher.handleLanguageSwitcher('Cancel');
            BVAnswerLanguagesSwitcher.handleLanguageSwitcher('Cancel');

            jQuery('#BVSubmissionQaContainer').empty();
            $('BVQAContainer').show();
        },
        doScrollSubmission: function() {
            $('BVSubmissionQaContainer').scrollTo();
            return false;
        },
        doShowContent: function() {
            var tabDt = jQuery('dt.tab-product\\.bv\\.qa').eq(0);
            if (tabDt &amp;&amp; !tabDt.hasClass('active')) {
                tabDt.trigger('click');
            }
        }
    });

    $BV.ui('qa', 'show_questions', {
        productId: '20061',
        subjectType: 'product',
        onEvent: function(json) {
            if ('Answer' === json.eventTarget) {
                BVAnswerLanguagesSwitcher.setParentId(json.attributes.ugcOnPage[0].id)
                        .handleLanguageSwitcher(json.pageType);
            } else {
                BVQuestionLanguagesSwitcher.handleLanguageSwitcher(json.pageType);
            }
        }
    });
      </script>
     </div>

         Please enter a valid email address. For example johndoe@domain.com.

      <script type="text/javascript">
       new UISlideform( document.getElementById( 'sb-email' ), 'email' );
    var newsFlag = window.location.hash.indexOf("newsletter");
    if(newsFlag == 1) {
        jQuery('#sb-email').css('display', 'none');
        jQuery('#Emailemail_msg').fadeOut('slow');
        jQuery('#nws-subscribed').fadeIn('slow');
    } else {
        jQuery('#nws-subscribed').fadeOut('slow');
    }
    function validationEmail(email) {
        jQuery('#Emailemail_msg').fadeOut('slow');
        var emailReg = /^[a-z0-9._%-+]+@[a-z0-9.-]+\.[a-z]{2,4}$/i;
        if(!emailReg.test( email ) || email == 'Email Address') {
            jQuery('#nws-subscribed').fadeOut('slow');
            jQuery('#Emailemail_msg').fadeIn('slow');
        } else if(email == '' || typeof email == 'undefined') {
            jQuery('#Emailemail_msg').fadeOut('slow');
        } else {
            jQuery('#Emailemail_msg').fadeOut('slow');
            jQuery('#mktForm_1182').submit();
        }
    }
      </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   jQuery(document).ready(function(){
    var outdatedBrowser = {
        box: jQuery("#outdatedbrowser"),
        shroud: jQuery("#ui-popup-overlay"),
        exit: jQuery("#outdatedbrowser .close"),
        browser: (function(){
            var N = navigator.appName, ua = navigator.userAgent, tem;
            var M = ua.match(/(opera|chrome|safari|firefox|msie)\/?\s*(\.?\d+(\.\d+)*)/i);
            if (M &amp;&amp; (tem= ua.match(/version\/([\.\d]+)/i))!= null) M[2]= tem[1];
            M = M ? [M[1], M[2]] : [N, navigator.appVersion, '-?'];
            return M;
        })(),
        hide: function() {
            this.box.removeClass("active");
            this.shroud.removeClass("active");
        },
        show: function() {
            this.box.addClass("active");
            this.shroud.addClass("active");
        },
        init: function() {
            if (
                (this.browser[0] == "Chrome" &amp;&amp; parseInt(this.browser[1], 10) &lt; 14)
                || (this.browser[0] == "Firefox" &amp;&amp; parseInt(this.browser[1], 10) &lt; 7)
                || (this.browser[0] == "MSIE" &amp;&amp; parseInt(this.browser[1], 10) &lt; 9)
                || (this.browser[0] == "Safari" &amp;&amp; parseInt(this.browser[1], 10) &lt; 5)
            ) {
                var self = this;
                this.exit.bind('click', function() {
                    document.cookie = "isUserAwareOfOutdatedBrowser=true; path=/magento-connect";
                    self.hide();
                });
                var value = false;
                var cookies = document.cookie;
                var pos = cookies.indexOf("isUserAwareOfOutdatedBrowser="); // {isUserAwareOfOutdatedBrowser=} 29 char
                if (pos != -1) {
                    var start = pos + 29;
                    var end = cookies.indexOf(";", start);
                    if (end == -1) {
                        end = cookies.length;
                    }
                    value = Boolean(cookies.substring(start, end));
                }
                if (!value) {
                    this.show();
                }
            }
        }
    }
    outdatedBrowser.init();
});
  </script>
